			if( cp_cookie != 'true' && cp_tcookie != 'true' ){
				var blueloop = setInterval(function() {
					console.log( 'info_bar in blue loop .. triggered flag = ' + info_bar_triggered_flag + ' & info_bar display: ' + info_bar.css('display') );
					if( info_bar_triggered_flag == false ){
						if( info_bar.css('display') == 'block' ){
							info_bar_triggered_flag = true;
							clearInterval( blueloop );
						} else {
							jQuery('#convertplus_trigger_63d6c').trigger('click');
						}
					}
				}, 1000 );
			} else { 
				console.log( "## SKIP BLUE LOOP ##" );
			}
			*/
			
		}
		
		function non_ad_block_user_action(){
			
			/*
			var cp_cookie = Cookies.get('cp_id_2a285');
			var cp_tcookie = Cookies.get('temp_cp_id_2a285');
			//var info_bar = jQuery('.cp-info-bar-container.cp-cp_id_2a285');
			var info_bar = jQuery('.cp-modal-popup-container.cp_id_2a285 .cp-overlay');
			var info_bar_triggered_flag = false;
			
			console.log( "RED LOOP: 2a285, cookie = "+cp_cookie+" & temp cookie = "+cp_tcookie );
			
			if( cp_cookie != 'true' && cp_tcookie != 'true' ){
				var redloop = setInterval(function() {
					console.log( 'info_bar in red loop .. triggered flag = ' + info_bar_triggered_flag + ' & info_bar display: ' + info_bar.css('display') );
					if( info_bar_triggered_flag == false ){
						if( info_bar.css('display') == 'block' ){

						}

				}, 1000 );
			} else { 
				console.log( "## SKIP RED LOOP ##" );
			}

		}
		
		function general_non_subscriber_action(){
			console.log( "## GENERAL NON AD BLOCKING USER ACTION ##" );
			non_ad_block_user_action();
		}
		
		if( subscription == 'active' ){
			
			console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ subscription cookie .. user is subscribed" );
			user_type = 'subscriber';
			subscribed_user_action();
			
		} else {
		
			console.log( '@@ ADMIRAL @@ connecting to API.');
			
			window.admiral = window.admiral || function() {(admiral.q = admiral.q || []).push(arguments)};
			
			window.admiral("after", "transact.subscribed", function(){
				
				console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ transact.subscribe .. user is subscribed");
				Cookies.set('rs_admiral_subscription', 'active', { expires: 7 });
				
				subscribed_user_action();
				user_type = 'subscriber';
				
			});
			
			window.admiral(	"after", "measure.detected", function( user ){ 
			
				if ( user.subscribed ) { 
					
					console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ measure.detected .. user is subscribed");
					Cookies.set('rs_admiral_subscription', 'active', { expires: 7 });
					subscribed_user_action();
					user_type = 'subscriber';
					
				} else if ( user.whitelisted ) {
					
					console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ measure.detected .. user is whitelisted");
					recovered_user_action();
					user_type = 'whitelisted';
						
				} else if ( user.adblocking ) { 
					
					console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ measure.detected .. user is adblocking");
					user_type = 'adblocking';
					
				} else {
					
					console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ on ready no ad blocking action triggered");
					user_type = 'general';
					//non_ad_block_user_action();
					
				}
				
				if( user_type != 'subscriber' ){
					general_non_subscriber_action();
				}
				
			});
			
		}
		
		
		Cookies.remove('cp_id_2fb37');
		
	</script>

							console.log( 'Flyout manage subscription link click' );
							window.location.href = 'https://my.getadmiral.com/';
							return false;
						});
						
					} else{
						
						/* Desktop Main Menu */
						
						jQuery('#menu-item-1507663').click( function(){
							console.log( 'Main Navi ad free login menu click' );
							window.admiral('show', 'transact.login');
							return false;
						});
						
						/* Mobile NAVI IN RED Main Menu */
						
						jQuery('#navi-in-red .mobile-ad-free-login-link').click( function(){
							console.log( 'Mobile ad free login menu click' );
							window.admiral('show', 'transact.login');
							return false;
						});
						
						/* Mobile FLYOUT Menu */
						
						jQuery('#menu-item-1517281').click( function(){

<div id="mvp-content-body" class="left relative">
<div id="mvp-content-body-top" class="left relative">
<div id="mvp-content-main" class="left relative 319">
<p>Appearing in CNN with host John King the Republican secretary of state for the state of Washington laughed at comments Donald Trump made during his Thursday night town hall where he predicted widespread voter fraud due to mail-in voting, saying she had no worries about it at all.</p>
<p>Speaking with host King, Secretary of State Kim Wyman was pressed to describe any problems she sees coming in November&#8217;s election.</p><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_incontent_p2' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center;  max-width: 728px;'><div class='ads_label' style='text-align: center; color: #ccc; font-size: 12px;'>ADVERTISEMENT</div><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_incontent_p2_google' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center;  max-width: 728px;'>

<div id='story_page_incontent_p2_target' class='min_height'></div>
<script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script type="text/javascript">
				
													
				var story_page_incontent_p2_code = "<div class='proper-ad-unit'>"+
										"<div id='proper-ad-rawstory_content_1'>"+
											"<scri"+"pt>propertag.cmd.push(function() { proper_display('rawstory_content_1'); });</scr"+"ipt>"+
										"</div>"+
									"</div>";
									
				var story_page_incontent_p2_target = jQuery( '#story_page_incontent_p2_target' );
				
				var width = jQuery(window).width();
				console.log( '@@story_page_incontent_p2@@ width: ' + width );
				
				if( width > 599 ){
					console.log( '@@story_page_incontent_p2@@ INJECT' );
					story_page_incontent_p2_target.html( story_page_incontent_p2_code );
				}			
				
			</script>
</div>
<div class="proper-ad-unit"><div id="proper-ad-rawstory_mobile_1"> <script> propertag.cmd.push(function() { proper_display('rawstory_mobile_1'); }); </script></div></div>
</div></p>
<p>&#8220;Kim Wyman thank you for your time again,&#8221; King began. &#8220;You&#8217;re the expert since you&#8217;ve been at it for so long in Washington. I was reading the transcript of an interview you did, you can handle this but what strikes you as the vitriol. You&#8217;re a Republican, but the nation&#8217;s top Republican is saying fraud, rigged, saying things that are frankly wrong, correct?&#8221;</p><div class='story_page_incontent_instagram_container story_page_incontent_ig'>
<div style='text-align: center; font-weight: bold; max-width: 490px; margin: 0 60px 0 86px;'>
<a id='incontent_ig_login_link' href='https://www.kindest.com/campaign/raw-story-podcast'>NEW! Help us launch the Raw Story Podcast. Click to learn more.</a></div></div></p>
<p>&#8220;That&#8217;s correct. and every time President Trump takes a swing at absentee ballots or vote-by-mail ballots it undermines confidence,&#8221; she replied. &#8220;So officials have more to do to make sure their voters know that their vote is protected, their vote is going to be counted accurately and we&#8217;re going to count for every vote we receive.&#8221;</p><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_incontent_p3' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center;  max-width: 600px;'>
<div>
<script id="02f2b5b0851a4fd0a7e10b8e510bc9e0">
				  cnx.cmd.push(function() {
					cnx({
					  playerId: '1e091718-9bec-4792-996d-0f25b35c582d'
					}).render('02f2b5b0851a4fd0a7e10b8e510bc9e0');
				  });
				</script>
</div>
</div></p>
<p>&#8216;The numbers the president was using with Savannah Guthrie were wrong, but there are cases where people are finding ballots discarded or in wrong locations. are other secretaries of state reaching out to you to how to handle it?&#8221; King asked. &#8220;Are you concerned so far? Do you think these are routine hiccups?&#8221;</p>
<p>&#8220;We&#8217;ve been working with secretaries of state and election officials from across the country for the last seven, eight months,&#8221; she explained. &#8220;10 percent rolls population moves every year so we&#8217;re trying to keep up our voter roles to make sure we have the most accurate address, get the ballot to the voter on the first try and the right ballot to the voter. But people move, and in an apartment or condominium we&#8217;ll have opportunities for people to receive someone else&#8217;s ballot that&#8217;s why we have security measures in place to make sure only the voter it was issued to gets to cast that ballot.&#8221;</p>
<p>&#8216;Your state is a high participation state anyway, a civic tradition and all that,&#8221; King continued. &#8220;I look at the primary turnout, number one and now the early questions: you have huge lines in many places with early voting. Based on those and based on your experience, what does it tell you about the interest in this election?&#8221;</p><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_incontent_p5' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center;  max-width: 550px;'><div class='ads_label' style='text-align: center; color: #ccc; font-size: 12px;'>ADVERTISEMENT</div>
<div class="teadsNative1 min_height"></div>
</div></p>
<p>&#8220;It&#8217;s exactly what we expected,&#8221; she replied. &#8220;We see very high turnout. I&#8217;m excited because I think what we&#8217;re going to see here in Washington is close to 90 percent turnout of our registered voters. As an election official, it makes you excited and we have to work really hard to make sure we get through all the volume.&#8221;</p>
<p>Watch below:</p>
<p><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/QoUqBBSsRSk" width="560" height="315" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen"></iframe></p>

news items that might have become controversies under another regime, but got buried  or were at least under-appreciated  due to the daily firehose of political pratfalls, unhinged tweet storms and other sundry embarrassments coming out of the current White House.</em></p><p>In the course of one week, we've moved from<em>The New York Post's</em> supposed "blockbuster" proving that Hunter Biden had arranged a meeting between an official with Burisma Holdings, the Ukrainian gas company whose board the younger Biden sat on, and then-Vice President Joe Biden to a contrived controversy over Twitter banning the story from its platform because it contained personal email addresses and phone numbers and we ended up with reports about Rudy Giuliani's apparent involvement in <a href="https://www.thedailybeast.com/man-who-reportedly-gave-hunters-laptop-to-rudy-speaks-out-in-bizarre-interview">a clumsy scheme to launder hacked emails</a> through a Seth Rich-truther at a computer shop, the likelihood that the emails were forged and <a href="https://apnews.com/article/election-2020-joe-biden-russia-024b553e9a4ffb2716286dd134876f8a">the FBI investigating the whole thing as a disinformation campaign</a> undertaken by foreign adversaries. It&#8217;s complicated</h1><div class="mvp-author-info-wrap left relative"><div class="mvp-author-info-thumb left relative"><img src='https://www.rawstory.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/salonsq.gif' data-no-lazy='true'></div><div class="mvp-author-info-text left relative"><div class="mvp-author-info-date left relative"><p>Published</p> <span class="mvp-post-date">3 hours ago</span> <p>on</p> <span class="mvp-post-date">October 17, 2020</span></div><div class="mvp-author-info-name left relative"><p>By</p> <span class="author-name vcard fn author 545" itemprop="name"><a href="https://www.rawstory.com/author/nicolek/" title="Posts by Nicole Karlis, Salon" rel="author">Nicole Karlis, Salon</a></span> </div></div></div></div><div class="mvp-post-add-body left relative"><div class="mvp-post-add-img left relative"><div id='pic_853102_3_ll_target' style='margin-top: 15px'></div><script type="text/javascript">var pic_853102_3_ll_code = "<picture><source media='(max-width: 479px)' srcset='https://www.rawstory.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/Bartender-Pouring-Drink-Shutterstock.jpg'><source media='(max-width: 360px)' srcset='https://www.rawstory.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/Bartender-Pouring-Drink-Shutterstock.jpg'><img src='https://www.rawstory.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/Bartender-Pouring-Drink-Shutterstock-1000x600.jpg' alt=''></picture>";var pic_853102_3_target = jQuery( '#pic_853102_3_ll_target' );var pic_853102_3_offset = pic_853102_3_target.offset();var pic_853102_3_ll_triggered_flag = false;var screen_height = jQuery( window ).height();jQuery(window).scroll(function() {var scroll_pos = jQuery(window).scrollTop();pic_853102_3_offset = pic_853102_3_target.offset();if( scroll_pos > ( pic_853102_3_offset.top - It's a question that's been on the mind of researchers, and the public alike. Humans often turn to alcohol in difficult times, which comes with its own problems: research shows that when you turn to drinking to cope with stress it's more likely to <a href="https://news.psu.edu/story/483248/2017/09/19/research/drinking-cope-stress-may-increase-risk-alcohol-problems">turn into a problem.</a>Yet as recently as last year, studies found that Americanmillennialsjust <a href="https://www.theatlantic.com/health/archive/2019/04/millennials-sober-sick-of-drinking/586186/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">weren't that into drinking</a>, perhaps because of related trends in wellness and healthy lifestyles.</div><div class="mvp-post-add-link"><a href="https://www.rawstory.com/2020/10/is-the-making-us-drink-more-or-less-its-complicated/" rel="bookmark"><span class="mvp-post-add-link-but">Continue Reading</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div>

<script>
					
					var container_1 = jQuery('#sticky-container_1');

					var container_offset_1 = container_1.offset();

					var sticky_start_point_1 = 0;

					function calculate_start_stop_1(){
						
						target_height_1 = target_1.height();
						
						container_offset_1 = container_1.offset();
						container_height_1 = container_1.height();
						
						sticky_start_point_1 = container_offset_1.top + 80;
						target_stop_offset_1 = container_height_1 - target_height_1 - 0;
						sticky_stop_point_1 = container_offset_1.top + target_stop_offset_1 - 80;
						
						var tmp_offset_1 = container_1.offset();
						scroll_offset_1 = tmp_offset_1.top - container_offset_1.top;
						offset_sticky_stop_point_1 = scroll_offset_1 + sticky_stop_point_1;
						
						/*
						console.log( '############    1    #############' );

					}
						
					jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
						
						if( window.innerWidth > 899 ){

							var scroll_pos_1 = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
							// console.log( 'Scroll position: ' + scroll_pos_1 );
							
							if ( scroll_pos_1 > sticky_start_point_1 && scroll_pos_1 < offset_sticky_stop_point_1 ){
								target_1.css('position','fixed');
								target_1.css('top','92px');
								// console.log( 'STICK 1' );
							} else if ( scroll_pos_1 < sticky_start_point_1 ){
								target_1.css('position','absolute');
								target_1.css('top','1px');
								// console.log( 'UNSTICK TOP 1' );

								target_1.css('position','absolute');

<script>
					
					var container_2 = jQuery('#sticky-container_2');
					var target_2 = jQuery('#sticky-target_2');
					
					// first need to determine when to start scrolling and when to stop
					var container_offset_2 = container_2.offset();
					var container_height_2 = container_2.height();
					
					var target_height_2 = 0;
					var sticky_start_point_2 = 0;
					var target_stop_offset_2 = 0;
					var sticky_stop_point_2 = 0;
					var scroll_offset_2 = 0;
					var offset_sticky_stop_point_2 = 0
					var scroll_offset_2 = 0;
					
					function calculate_start_stop_2(){
						
						target_height_2 = target_2.height();
						
						container_offset_2 = container_2.offset();
						container_height_2 = container_2.height();
						
						sticky_start_point_2 = container_offset_2.top + 80;
						target_stop_offset_2 = container_height_2 - target_height_2 - 0;
						sticky_stop_point_2 = container_offset_2.top + target_stop_offset_2 - 80;
						
						var tmp_offset_2 = container_2.offset();
						scroll_offset_2 = tmp_offset_2.top - container_offset_2.top;
						offset_sticky_stop_point_2 = scroll_offset_2 + sticky_stop_point_2;
						
						/*
						console.log( '############    2    #############' );
						console.log( 'Scroll offset: ' + scroll_offset_2 );
						console.log( 'target height ' + target_height_2 );
						console.log( 'container_offset.top ' + container_offset_2.top );
						console.log( 'target_stop_offset ' + target_stop_offset_2 );
						console.log( 'start scrolling with page at ' + sticky_start_point_2 );
						console.log( 'stop scrolling with page at ' + offset_sticky_stop_point_2 );
						*/
					}
						
					jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
						
						if( window.innerWidth > 899 ){
							
							calculate_start_stop_2();
							
							var scroll_pos_2 = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
							// console.log( 'Scroll position: ' + scroll_pos_2 );
							
							if ( scroll_pos_2 > sticky_start_point_2 && scroll_pos_2 < offset_sticky_stop_point_2 ){
								target_2.css('position','fixed');
								target_2.css('top','92px');
								// console.log( 'STICK 1' );
							} else if ( scroll_pos_2 < sticky_start_point_2 ){
								target_2.css('position','absolute');
								target_2.css('top','1px');
								// console.log( 'UNSTICK TOP 1' );
							} else if ( scroll_pos_2 > offset_sticky_stop_point_2 ){
								target_2.css('position','absolute');
								target_2.css('top', target_stop_offset_2+'px');
								// console.log( "UNSTICK BOTTOM 1" );
							}

						} else {
							
							jQuery(window).scroll(function(){
								//console.log( 'container 1 height: ' + container_2.height() );
								//console.log( 'target 1 height: ' + target_2.height() );
								container_2.css( 'height' , target_2.height() );
							});
							
						}
						
					});
						
				</script>

				function stopclock (){
					if(timerRunning) clearTimeout(timerID);
					timerRunning = false;
						//document.cookie="time=0";
					}
					function showtime () {
						var now = new Date();
						var my = now.getTime() ;
						now = new Date(my-diffms) ;
						//document.cookie="time="+now.toLocaleString();
						timerID = setTimeout('showtime()',10000);
						timerRunning = true;
					}
					function startclock () {
						stopclock();
						showtime();
					}

					var timerRunning = false;

<script type='text/javascript'>
	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	$(window).load(function(){
	var leaderHeight = $("#mvp-leader-wrap").outerHeight();
	var logoHeight = $("#mvp-main-nav-top").outerHeight();
	var botHeight = $("#mvp-main-nav-bot").outerHeight();
	var navHeight = $("#mvp-main-head-wrap").outerHeight();
	var headerHeight = navHeight + leaderHeight;
	var aboveNav = leaderHeight + logoHeight;
	var totalHeight = logoHeight + botHeight;
	var previousScroll = 0;
	$(window).scroll(function(event){
			var scroll = $(this).scrollTop();
			if ($(window).scrollTop() > aboveNav){
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-nav-small");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").css("margin-top", logoHeight );
			} else {
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-nav-small");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").css("margin-top","0");
			}
			if ($(window).scrollTop() > headerHeight){
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-fixed");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").addClass("mvp-fixed1");
				$("#mvp-main-body-wrap").css("margin-top", totalHeight );
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-fixed-shadow");
				$(".mvp-nav-top-mid").addClass("mvp-fixed-post");
				$(".mvp-drop-nav-title").show();
				$(".mvp-fly-top").addClass("mvp-to-top");
				

				$("#menu-left-message-container").css("height","19px").css("margin-top","-6px");
				$("#menu-left-button-container-subscribe").hide();


	    		if(scroll < previousScroll) {
					$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").addClass("mvp-fixed2");
					$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-fixed-shadow");
					$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-soc-mob-up");
					$("#mvp-soc-mob-wrap").removeClass("mvp-soc-mob-up");
				} else {
					$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").removeClass("mvp-fixed2");
					$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-fixed-shadow");
					$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-soc-mob-up");
					$("#mvp-soc-mob-wrap").addClass("mvp-soc-mob-up");
				}
			} else {
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-fixed");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").removeClass("mvp-fixed1");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").removeClass("mvp-fixed2");
				$("#mvp-main-body-wrap").css("margin-top","0");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-fixed-shadow");
				$(".mvp-nav-top-mid").removeClass("mvp-fixed-post");
				$(".mvp-drop-nav-title").hide();
	    		$(".mvp-fly-top").removeClass("mvp-to-top");
				
			
				$("#menu-left-message-container").css("height","40px").css("margin-top","-15px");
				$("#menu-left-button-container-subscribe").show();

			}
			previousScroll = scroll;
	});
	});
	});
	

	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	// Video Post Scroll
	$(window).on("scroll.video", function(event){
		var scrollTop     = $(window).scrollTop();
    	var elementOffset = $("#mvp-content-wrap").offset().top;
    	var distance      = (elementOffset - scrollTop);
		var aboveHeight = $("#mvp-video-embed-wrap").outerHeight();
		if ($(window).scrollTop() > distance + aboveHeight + screen.height){
			$("#mvp-video-embed-cont").addClass("mvp-vid-fixed");
			$("#mvp-video-embed-wrap").addClass("mvp-vid-height");
			$(".mvp-video-close").show();
		} else {
			$("#mvp-video-embed-cont").removeClass("mvp-vid-fixed");
			$("#mvp-video-embed-wrap").removeClass("mvp-vid-height");
			$(".mvp-video-close").hide();
		}
	});

 	$(".mvp-video-close").on("click", function(){
		$("iframe").attr("src", $("iframe").attr("src"));
		$("#mvp-video-embed-cont").removeClass("mvp-vid-fixed");
		$("#mvp-video-embed-wrap").removeClass("mvp-vid-height");
		$(".mvp-video-close").hide();
		$(window).off("scroll.video");
  	});

	});

	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	$(".menu-item-has-children a").click(function(event){
	  event.stopPropagation();
	  
  	});

	$(".menu-item-has-children").click(function(){
    	  $(this).addClass("toggled");
    	  if($(".menu-item-has-children").hasClass("toggled"))
    	  {
    	  $(this).children("ul").toggle();

    	  return false;
  	});

<script>
var hideCpInfoBarAll = Cookies.get('hide-cp-info-bar-all'); 

setTimeout(function() {
	// info-bar
	if (screen.width > 374 && hideCpInfoBarAll != 'true') {
		document.getElementById('cp-info-bar-all').style.display = 'inline';
		document.getElementById('ib-img-close-all').addEventListener('click', handleClose);
		document.getElementById('cp-submit-link-all').addEventListener('click', handleClick);   	
		document.getElementById('cp-submit-button-all').addEventListener('click', handleClick);   	
	}
	
	function handleClose(e){
		var cookieExpirateTime = 0;
		e.target.id == 'ib-img-close-all' ? cookieExpirateTime = 3 : cookieExpirateTime = 14
		document.getElementById('cp-info-bar-all').style.display = 'none';
		Cookies.set('hide-cp-info-bar-all', 'true', { expires: cookieExpirateTime });
	};

	function handleClick(e){
		var cookieExpirateTime = 0;
		e.target.id == 'ib-img-close-all' ? cookieExpirateTime = 3 : cookieExpirateTime = 14
		document.getElementById('cp-info-bar-all').style.display = 'none';
		Cookies.set('hide-cp-info-bar-all', 'true', { expires: cookieExpirateTime });
		window.location.href = "https://www.rawstory.com/raw-story-investigates-invest-in-pulitzer-prizen-driven-journalism-to-make-a-difference-in-2020/";
	};
	
}, 1000);
</script>

			} else { 
				console.log( "## SKIP BLUE LOOP ##" );
			}
			*/
			
		}
		
		function non_ad_block_user_action(){
			
			/*
			var cp_cookie = Cookies.get('cp_id_2a285');
			var cp_tcookie = Cookies.get('temp_cp_id_2a285');
			//var info_bar = jQuery('.cp-info-bar-container.cp-cp_id_2a285');
			var info_bar = jQuery('.cp-modal-popup-container.cp_id_2a285 .cp-overlay');
			var info_bar_triggered_flag = false;
			
			console.log( "RED LOOP: 2a285, cookie = "+cp_cookie+" & temp cookie = "+cp_tcookie );
			
			if( cp_cookie != 'true' && cp_tcookie != 'true' ){
				var redloop = setInterval(function() {
					console.log( 'info_bar in red loop .. triggered flag = ' + info_bar_triggered_flag + ' & info_bar display: ' + info_bar.css('display') );
					if( info_bar_triggered_flag == false ){
						if( info_bar.css('display') == 'block' ){
							info_bar_triggered_flag = true;
							clearInterval( redloop );
						} else {
							jQuery('#convertplus_trigger_2a285').trigger('click');
						}
					}
				}, 1000 );
			} else { 
				console.log( "## SKIP RED LOOP ##" );
			}
			*/

		}
		
		function general_non_subscriber_action(){
			console.log( "## GENERAL NON AD BLOCKING USER ACTION ##" );
			non_ad_block_user_action();
		}
		
		if( subscription == 'active' ){
			
			console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ subscription cookie .. user is subscribed" );
			user_type = 'subscriber';
			subscribed_user_action();
			
		} else {
		
			console.log( '@@ ADMIRAL @@ connecting to API.');
			
			window.admiral = window.admiral || function() {(admiral.q = admiral.q || []).push(arguments)};
			
			window.admiral("after", "transact.subscribed", function(){
				
				console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ transact.subscribe .. user is subscribed");
				Cookies.set('rs_admiral_subscription', 'active', { expires: 7 });
				
				subscribed_user_action();
				user_type = 'subscriber';
				
			});
			
			window.admiral(	"after", "measure.detected", function( user ){ 
			
				if ( user.subscribed ) { 
					
					console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ measure.detected .. user is subscribed");
					Cookies.set('rs_admiral_subscription', 'active', { expires: 7 });
					subscribed_user_action();
					user_type = 'subscriber';
					
				} else if ( user.whitelisted ) {
					
					console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ measure.detected .. user is whitelisted");
					recovered_user_action();
					user_type = 'whitelisted';
						
				} else if ( user.adblocking ) { 
					
					console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ measure.detected .. user is adblocking");
					user_type = 'adblocking';
					
				} else {
					
					console.log( "@@ ADMIRAL @@ on ready no ad blocking action triggered");
					user_type = 'general';
					//non_ad_block_user_action();
					
				}
				
				if( user_type != 'subscriber' ){
					general_non_subscriber_action();
				}
				
			});
			
		}
		
		
		Cookies.remove('cp_id_2fb37');
		
	</script>

						jQuery('#menu-item-1517281').click( function(){
							console.log( 'Flyout ad free login menu click' );
							window.admiral('show', 'transact.login');
							return false;
						});
						
					}

<div id="mvp-content-body" class="left relative">
<div id="mvp-content-body-top" class="left relative">
<div id="mvp-content-main" class="left relative 319">
<p>Appearing in CNN with host John King the Republican secretary of state for the state of Washington laughed at comments Donald Trump made during his Thursday night town hall where he predicted widespread voter fraud due to mail-in voting, saying she had no worries about it at all.</p>
<p>Speaking with host King, Secretary of State Kim Wyman was pressed to describe any problems she sees coming in November&#8217;s election.</p><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_incontent_p2' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center;  max-width: 728px;'><div class='ads_label' style='text-align: center; color: #ccc; font-size: 12px;'>ADVERTISEMENT</div><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_incontent_p2_google' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center;  max-width: 728px;'>

<div id='story_page_incontent_p2_target' class='min_height'></div>
<script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script type="text/javascript">
				
													
				var story_page_incontent_p2_code = "<div class='proper-ad-unit'>"+
										"<div id='proper-ad-rawstory_content_1'>"+
											"<scri"+"pt>propertag.cmd.push(function() { proper_display('rawstory_content_1'); });</scr"+"ipt>"+
										"</div>"+
									"</div>";
									
				var story_page_incontent_p2_target = jQuery( '#story_page_incontent_p2_target' );
				
				var width = jQuery(window).width();
				console.log( '@@story_page_incontent_p2@@ width: ' + width );
				
				if( width > 599 ){
					console.log( '@@story_page_incontent_p2@@ INJECT' );
					story_page_incontent_p2_target.html( story_page_incontent_p2_code );
				}			
				
			</script>
</div>
<div class="proper-ad-unit"><div id="proper-ad-rawstory_mobile_1"> <script> propertag.cmd.push(function() { proper_display('rawstory_mobile_1'); }); </script></div></div>
</div></p>
<p>&#8220;Kim Wyman thank you for your time again,&#8221; King began. &#8220;You&#8217;re the expert since you&#8217;ve been at it for so long in Washington. I was reading the transcript of an interview you did, you can handle this but what strikes you as the vitriol. You&#8217;re a Republican, but the nation&#8217;s top Republican is saying fraud, rigged, saying things that are frankly wrong, correct?&#8221;</p><div class='story_page_incontent_instagram_container story_page_incontent_ig'>
<div style='text-align: center; font-weight: bold; max-width: 490px; margin: 0 60px 0 86px;'>
<a id='incontent_ig_login_link' href='https://www.kindest.com/campaign/raw-story-podcast'>NEW! Help us launch the Raw Story Podcast. Click to learn more.</a></div></div></p>
<p>&#8220;That&#8217;s correct. and every time President Trump takes a swing at absentee ballots or vote-by-mail ballots it undermines confidence,&#8221; she replied. &#8220;So officials have more to do to make sure their voters know that their vote is protected, their vote is going to be counted accurately and we&#8217;re going to count for every vote we receive.&#8221;</p><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_incontent_p3' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center;  max-width: 600px;'>
<div>
<script id="02f2b5b0851a4fd0a7e10b8e510bc9e0">
				  cnx.cmd.push(function() {
					cnx({
					  playerId: '1e091718-9bec-4792-996d-0f25b35c582d'
					}).render('02f2b5b0851a4fd0a7e10b8e510bc9e0');
				  });
				</script>
</div>
</div></p>
<p>&#8216;The numbers the president was using with Savannah Guthrie were wrong, but there are cases where people are finding ballots discarded or in wrong locations. are other secretaries of state reaching out to you to how to handle it?&#8221; King asked. &#8220;Are you concerned so far? Do you think these are routine hiccups?&#8221;</p>
<p>&#8220;We&#8217;ve been working with secretaries of state and election officials from across the country for the last seven, eight months,&#8221; she explained. &#8220;10 percent rolls population moves every year so we&#8217;re trying to keep up our voter roles to make sure we have the most accurate address, get the ballot to the voter on the first try and the right ballot to the voter. But people move, and in an apartment or condominium we&#8217;ll have opportunities for people to receive someone else&#8217;s ballot that&#8217;s why we have security measures in place to make sure only the voter it was issued to gets to cast that ballot.&#8221;</p>
<p>&#8216;Your state is a high participation state anyway, a civic tradition and all that,&#8221; King continued. &#8220;I look at the primary turnout, number one and now the early questions: you have huge lines in many places with early voting. Based on those and based on your experience, what does it tell you about the interest in this election?&#8221;</p><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_incontent_p5' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center;  max-width: 550px;'><div class='ads_label' style='text-align: center; color: #ccc; font-size: 12px;'>ADVERTISEMENT</div>
<div class="teadsNative1 min_height"></div>
</div></p>
<p>&#8220;It&#8217;s exactly what we expected,&#8221; she replied. &#8220;We see very high turnout. I&#8217;m excited because I think what we&#8217;re going to see here in Washington is close to 90 percent turnout of our registered voters. As an election official, it makes you excited and we have to work really hard to make sure we get through all the volume.&#8221;</p>
<p>Watch below:</p>
<p><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/QoUqBBSsRSk" width="560" height="315" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen"></iframe></p>

true;}}});</script></div><div class="mvp-post-add-cont left relative"><div class="mvp-post-add-main right relative"><p><em>Welcome to another edition of What Fresh Hell?,</em>Raw Story<em>s roundup of news items that might have become controversies under another regime, but got buried  or were at least under-appreciated  due to the daily firehose of political pratfalls, unhinged tweet storms and other sundry embarrassments coming out of the current White House.</em></p><p>In the course of one week, we've moved from<em>The New York Post's</em> supposed "blockbuster" proving that Hunter Biden had arranged a meeting between an official with Burisma Holdings, the Ukrainian gas company whose board the younger Biden sat on, and then-Vice President Joe Biden to a contrived controversy over Twitter banning the story from its platform because it contained personal email addresses and phone numbers and we ended up with reports about Rudy Giuliani's apparent involvement in <a href="https://www.thedailybeast.com/man-who-reportedly-gave-hunters-laptop-to-rudy-speaks-out-in-bizarre-interview">a clumsy scheme to launder hacked emails</a> through a Seth Rich-truther at a computer shop, the likelihood that the emails were forged and <a href="https://apnews.com/article/election-2020-joe-biden-russia-024b553e9a4ffb2716286dd134876f8a">the FBI investigating the whole thing as a disinformation campaign</a> undertaken by foreign adversaries. When they rolled out the "story" on Monday, they probably didn't expect headlines like "<a href="https://www.thedailybeast.com/rudy-giuliani-says-theres-only-5050-chance-i-worked-with-a-russian-spy-to-dig-dirt-on-bidens?scrolla=5eb6d68b7fedc32c19ef33b4">Rudy: Only 50/50 Chance I Worked With a Russian Spy to Dig Dirt on Bidens</a>" to be prevalent by Saturday.</div><div class="mvp-post-add-link"><a href="https://www.rawstory.com/2020/10/trump-worlds-desperate-hunter-biden-pseudo-scandal-backfired-on-them-in-record-time/" rel="bookmark"><span class="mvp-post-add-link-but">Continue Reading</span></a></div></div></div><div class='clear: both;'>&nbsp;</div><div class='rs_ad_block story_page_add_wrap_after_2' style='margin: 0 auto; text-align: center; margin-top: 10px;'><div class="proper-ad-unit" style='min-height: 90px;'></div><div id="proper-ad-rawstory_content_10"> <script> propertag.cmd.push(function() { proper_display('rawstory_content_10'); }); </script> </div></div></div></div><div id="add-wrap-post-1677605" class="mvp-post-add-story left relative add-wrap-count-3 add-wrap-cat-2020-election add-wrap-post-1677605"><div class="mvp-post-add-head left relative"><h3 class="mvp-post-cat left relative"><a class="mvp-post-cat-link 517" href="https://www.rawstory.com/category/2020-election/"><span class="mvp-post-cat left">2020 Election</span></a></h3><h1 class="mvp-post-title left">Is the pandemic making us drink more, or less? It&#8217;s complicated</h1><div class="mvp-author-info-wrap left relative"><div class="mvp-author-info-thumb left relative"><img src='https://www.rawstory.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/salonsq.gif' data-no-lazy='true'></div><div class="mvp-author-info-text left relative"><div class="mvp-author-info-date left relative"><p>Published</p> <span class="mvp-post-date">3 hours ago</span> <p>on</p> <span class="mvp-post-date">October 17, 2020</span></div><div class="mvp-author-info-name left relative"><p>By</p> <span class="author-name vcard fn author 545" itemprop="name"><a href="https://www.rawstory.com/author/nicolek/" title="Posts by Nicole Karlis, Salon" rel="author">Nicole Karlis, Salon</a></span> </div></div></div></div><div class="mvp-post-add-body left relative"><div class="mvp-post-add-img left relative"><div id='pic_853102_3_ll_target' style='margin-top: 15px'></div><script type="text/javascript">var pic_853102_3_ll_code = "<picture><source media='(max-width: 479px)' srcset='https://www.rawstory.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/Bartender-Pouring-Drink-Shutterstock.jpg'><source media='(max-width: 360px)' srcset='https://www.rawstory.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/Bartender-Pouring-Drink-Shutterstock.jpg'><img src='https://www.rawstory.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/Bartender-Pouring-Drink-Shutterstock-1000x600.jpg' alt=''></picture>";var pic_853102_3_target = jQuery( '#pic_853102_3_ll_target' );var pic_853102_3_offset = pic_853102_3_target.offset();var pic_853102_3_ll_triggered_flag = false;var screen_height = jQuery( window ).height();jQuery(window).scroll(function() {var scroll_pos = jQuery(window).scrollTop();pic_853102_3_offset = pic_853102_3_target.offset();if( scroll_pos > ( pic_853102_3_offset.top - It's a question that's been on the mind of researchers, and the public alike. Humans often turn to alcohol in difficult times, which comes with its own problems: research shows that when you turn to drinking to cope with stress it's more likely to <a href="https://news.psu.edu/story/483248/2017/09/19/research/drinking-cope-stress-may-increase-risk-alcohol-problems">turn into a problem.</a>Yet as recently as last year, studies found that Americanmillennialsjust <a href="https://www.theatlantic.com/health/archive/2019/04/millennials-sober-sick-of-drinking/586186/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">weren't that into drinking</a>, perhaps because of related trends in wellness and healthy lifestyles.</div><div class="mvp-post-add-link"><a href="https://www.rawstory.com/2020/10/is-the-making-us-drink-more-or-less-its-complicated/" rel="bookmark"><span class="mvp-post-add-link-but">Continue Reading</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div>

	function fire_disqus() {

		var dsq = document.createElement('script'); dsq.type = 'text/javascript';
		dsq.async = true;
		dsq.src = '//' + disqus_shortname + '.disqus.com/embed.js';
		(document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0] || document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0]).appendChild(dsq);
	}
						
	var disqus_target = jQuery( '#disqus_thread' );
	var disqus_offset = disqus_target.offset();
	var disqus_ll_triggered_flag = false;
	var screen_height = jQuery( window ).height();
	jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
		var scroll_pos = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
		disqus_offset = disqus_target.offset();
		
		if( scroll_pos > ( disqus_offset.top - ( screen_height * 3 ) ) ) {
			if(  disqus_ll_triggered_flag == false ){
				console.log( "### FIRED lazy load disqus ###" );
				fire_disqus();
				disqus_ll_triggered_flag = true;
			}
		}
		
	});
	
</script>

<script>
					
					var container_1 = jQuery('#sticky-container_1');
					var target_1 = jQuery('#sticky-target_1');
					
					// first need to determine when to start scrolling and when to stop
					var container_offset_1 = container_1.offset();
					var container_height_1 = container_1.height();
					
					var target_height_1 = 0;
					var sticky_start_point_1 = 0;
					var target_stop_offset_1 = 0;
					var sticky_stop_point_1 = 0;
					var scroll_offset_1 = 0;
					var offset_sticky_stop_point_1 = 0
					var scroll_offset_1 = 0;
					
					function calculate_start_stop_1(){
						
						target_height_1 = target_1.height();
						
						container_offset_1 = container_1.offset();
						container_height_1 = container_1.height();
						
						sticky_start_point_1 = container_offset_1.top + 80;
						target_stop_offset_1 = container_height_1 - target_height_1 - 0;
						sticky_stop_point_1 = container_offset_1.top + target_stop_offset_1 - 80;
						
						var tmp_offset_1 = container_1.offset();
						scroll_offset_1 = tmp_offset_1.top - container_offset_1.top;
						offset_sticky_stop_point_1 = scroll_offset_1 + sticky_stop_point_1;
						
						/*
						console.log( '############    1    #############' );
						console.log( 'Scroll offset: ' + scroll_offset_1 );
						console.log( 'target height ' + target_height_1 );
						console.log( 'container_offset.top ' + container_offset_1.top );
						console.log( 'target_stop_offset ' + target_stop_offset_1 );
						console.log( 'start scrolling with page at ' + sticky_start_point_1 );
						console.log( 'stop scrolling with page at ' + offset_sticky_stop_point_1 );
						*/
					}
						
					jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
						
						if( window.innerWidth > 899 ){
							
							calculate_start_stop_1();
							
							var scroll_pos_1 = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
							// console.log( 'Scroll position: ' + scroll_pos_1 );
							
							if ( scroll_pos_1 > sticky_start_point_1 && scroll_pos_1 < offset_sticky_stop_point_1 ){
								target_1.css('position','fixed');
								target_1.css('top','92px');
								// console.log( 'STICK 1' );
							} else if ( scroll_pos_1 < sticky_start_point_1 ){
								target_1.css('position','absolute');
								target_1.css('top','1px');
								// console.log( 'UNSTICK TOP 1' );
							} else if ( scroll_pos_1 > offset_sticky_stop_point_1 ){
								target_1.css('position','absolute');
								target_1.css('top', target_stop_offset_1+'px');
								// console.log( "UNSTICK BOTTOM 1" );
							}

						} else {
							
							jQuery(window).scroll(function(){
								//console.log( 'container 1 height: ' + container_1.height() );
								//console.log( 'target 1 height: ' + target_1.height() );
								container_1.css( 'height' , target_1.height() );
							});
							
						}
						
					});

<script>
					
					var container_2 = jQuery('#sticky-container_2');
					var target_2 = jQuery('#sticky-target_2');
					
					// first need to determine when to start scrolling and when to stop
					var container_offset_2 = container_2.offset();
					var container_height_2 = container_2.height();
					
					var target_height_2 = 0;
					var sticky_start_point_2 = 0;
					var target_stop_offset_2 = 0;
					var sticky_stop_point_2 = 0;
					var scroll_offset_2 = 0;
					var offset_sticky_stop_point_2 = 0
					var scroll_offset_2 = 0;
					
					function calculate_start_stop_2(){
						
						target_height_2 = target_2.height();
						
						container_offset_2 = container_2.offset();
						container_height_2 = container_2.height();
						
						sticky_start_point_2 = container_offset_2.top + 80;
						target_stop_offset_2 = container_height_2 - target_height_2 - 0;
						sticky_stop_point_2 = container_offset_2.top + target_stop_offset_2 - 80;
						
						var tmp_offset_2 = container_2.offset();
						scroll_offset_2 = tmp_offset_2.top - container_offset_2.top;
						offset_sticky_stop_point_2 = scroll_offset_2 + sticky_stop_point_2;
						
						/*
						console.log( '############    2    #############' );
						console.log( 'Scroll offset: ' + scroll_offset_2 );
						console.log( 'target height ' + target_height_2 );
						console.log( 'container_offset.top ' + container_offset_2.top );
						console.log( 'target_stop_offset ' + target_stop_offset_2 );
						console.log( 'start scrolling with page at ' + sticky_start_point_2 );
						console.log( 'stop scrolling with page at ' + offset_sticky_stop_point_2 );
						*/
					}
						
					jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
						
						if( window.innerWidth > 899 ){
							
							calculate_start_stop_2();
							
							var scroll_pos_2 = jQuery(window).scrollTop();
							// console.log( 'Scroll position: ' + scroll_pos_2 );
							
							if ( scroll_pos_2 > sticky_start_point_2 && scroll_pos_2 < offset_sticky_stop_point_2 ){
								target_2.css('position','fixed');
								target_2.css('top','92px');
								// console.log( 'STICK 1' );
							} else if ( scroll_pos_2 < sticky_start_point_2 ){
								target_2.css('position','absolute');
								target_2.css('top','1px');
								// console.log( 'UNSTICK TOP 1' );
							} else if ( scroll_pos_2 > offset_sticky_stop_point_2 ){
								target_2.css('position','absolute');
								target_2.css('top', target_stop_offset_2+'px');
								// console.log( "UNSTICK BOTTOM 1" );
							}

						} else {
							
							jQuery(window).scroll(function(){
								//console.log( 'container 1 height: ' + container_2.height() );
								//console.log( 'target 1 height: ' + target_2.height() );
								container_2.css( 'height' , target_2.height() );
							});
							
						}
						
					});
						
				</script>

	window.onscroll = function(ev) {
		
		var ccpa_button = jQuery('.fc-ccpa-root');
		var footer_offset_top = jQuery('#mvp-foot-top').offset().top - ( window.innerHeight * .75 );

    	if ( ( window.scrollY) >= footer_offset_top ) {
			ccpa_button.attr('style','opacity: .99 !important;');

			ccpa_button.attr('style','opacity: .00 !important;');
		}

	};

				function stopclock (){
					if(timerRunning) clearTimeout(timerID);
					timerRunning = false;
						//document.cookie="time=0";
					}
					function showtime () {
						var now = new Date();
						var my = now.getTime() ;
						now = new Date(my-diffms) ;
						//document.cookie="time="+now.toLocaleString();
						timerID = setTimeout('showtime()',10000);
						timerRunning = true;
					}
					function startclock () {
						stopclock();
						showtime();
					}

					var timerRunning = false;
					var x = new Date() ;

<script type='text/javascript'>
	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	$(window).load(function(){
	var leaderHeight = $("#mvp-leader-wrap").outerHeight();
	var logoHeight = $("#mvp-main-nav-top").outerHeight();
	var botHeight = $("#mvp-main-nav-bot").outerHeight();
	var navHeight = $("#mvp-main-head-wrap").outerHeight();
	var headerHeight = navHeight + leaderHeight;
	var aboveNav = leaderHeight + logoHeight;
	var totalHeight = logoHeight + botHeight;
	var previousScroll = 0;
	$(window).scroll(function(event){
			var scroll = $(this).scrollTop();
			if ($(window).scrollTop() > aboveNav){
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-nav-small");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").css("margin-top", logoHeight );
			} else {
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-nav-small");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").css("margin-top","0");
			}
			if ($(window).scrollTop() > headerHeight){
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-fixed");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").addClass("mvp-fixed1");
				$("#mvp-main-body-wrap").css("margin-top", totalHeight );
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-fixed-shadow");
				$(".mvp-nav-top-mid").addClass("mvp-fixed-post");
				$(".mvp-drop-nav-title").show();
				$(".mvp-fly-top").addClass("mvp-to-top");
				

				$("#menu-left-message-container").css("height","19px").css("margin-top","-6px");
				$("#menu-left-button-container-subscribe").hide();


	    		if(scroll < previousScroll) {
					$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").addClass("mvp-fixed2");
					$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-fixed-shadow");
					$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-soc-mob-up");
					$("#mvp-soc-mob-wrap").removeClass("mvp-soc-mob-up");
				} else {
					$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").removeClass("mvp-fixed2");
					$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-fixed-shadow");
					$("#mvp-main-nav-top").addClass("mvp-soc-mob-up");
					$("#mvp-soc-mob-wrap").addClass("mvp-soc-mob-up");
				}
			} else {
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-fixed");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").removeClass("mvp-fixed1");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-bot").removeClass("mvp-fixed2");
				$("#mvp-main-body-wrap").css("margin-top","0");
				$("#mvp-main-nav-top").removeClass("mvp-fixed-shadow");
				$(".mvp-nav-top-mid").removeClass("mvp-fixed-post");
				$(".mvp-drop-nav-title").hide();
	    		$(".mvp-fly-top").removeClass("mvp-to-top");
				
			
				$("#menu-left-message-container").css("height","40px").css("margin-top","-15px");
				$("#menu-left-button-container-subscribe").show();

			}
			previousScroll = scroll;
	});
	});
	});
	

	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	// Video Post Scroll
	$(window).on("scroll.video", function(event){
		var scrollTop     = $(window).scrollTop();
    	var elementOffset = $("#mvp-content-wrap").offset().top;
    	var distance      = (elementOffset - scrollTop);
		var aboveHeight = $("#mvp-video-embed-wrap").outerHeight();
		if ($(window).scrollTop() > distance + aboveHeight + screen.height){
			$("#mvp-video-embed-cont").addClass("mvp-vid-fixed");
			$("#mvp-video-embed-wrap").addClass("mvp-vid-height");
			$(".mvp-video-close").show();
		} else {
			$("#mvp-video-embed-cont").removeClass("mvp-vid-fixed");
			$("#mvp-video-embed-wrap").removeClass("mvp-vid-height");
			$(".mvp-video-close").hide();
		}
	});

 	$(".mvp-video-close").on("click", function(){
		$("iframe").attr("src", $("iframe").attr("src"));
		$("#mvp-video-embed-cont").removeClass("mvp-vid-fixed");
		$("#mvp-video-embed-wrap").removeClass("mvp-vid-height");
		$(".mvp-video-close").hide();
		$(window).off("scroll.video");
  	});

	});

	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	$(".menu-item-has-children a").click(function(event){
	  event.stopPropagation();
	  
  	});

	$(".menu-item-has-children").click(function(){
    	  $(this).addClass("toggled");
    	  if($(".menu-item-has-children").hasClass("toggled"))
    	  {
    	  $(this).children("ul").toggle();
	  $(".mvp-fly-nav-menu").getNiceScroll().resize();
	  }
	  $(this).toggleClass("tog-minus");
    	  return false;
  	});

	// Main Menu Scroll

	});

	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
	$(".infinite-content").infinitescroll({
	  navSelector: ".mvp-nav-links",

                                image_count += 1;
                            }

                            if(is_iframe){
                                iframe_count += 1;
                            }
                        }
                    } );

                        lazyLoadInstance.update();
                    }
                } );

<script>
var hideCpInfoBarAll = Cookies.get('hide-cp-info-bar-all'); 

setTimeout(function() {
	// info-bar
	if (screen.width > 374 && hideCpInfoBarAll != 'true') {
		document.getElementById('cp-info-bar-all').style.display = 'inline';
		document.getElementById('ib-img-close-all').addEventListener('click', handleClose);
		document.getElementById('cp-submit-link-all').addEventListener('click', handleClick);   	
		document.getElementById('cp-submit-button-all').addEventListener('click', handleClick);   	
	}
	
	function handleClose(e){
		var cookieExpirateTime = 0;
		e.target.id == 'ib-img-close-all' ? cookieExpirateTime = 3 : cookieExpirateTime = 14
		document.getElementById('cp-info-bar-all').style.display = 'none';
		Cookies.set('hide-cp-info-bar-all', 'true', { expires: cookieExpirateTime });
	};

	function handleClick(e){
		var cookieExpirateTime = 0;
		e.target.id == 'ib-img-close-all' ? cookieExpirateTime = 3 : cookieExpirateTime = 14
		document.getElementById('cp-info-bar-all').style.display = 'none';
		Cookies.set('hide-cp-info-bar-all', 'true', { expires: cookieExpirateTime });
		window.location.href = "https://www.rawstory.com/raw-story-investigates-invest-in-pulitzer-prizen-driven-journalism-to-make-a-difference-in-2020/";
	};
	
}, 1000);
</script>
